Nigiri is authentic and is truly amazing. Fresh fish, great texture, beautiful fillets... Also, skewered chicken is delicious. I was born and raised in Japan and moved to the states 5 years ago. I had never been satisfied with sushi abroad but now I found this place! Personally, it was lucky to find my favorite Japanese red snapper as it is very hard to find authentic one. I really enjoyed foods here, and I'd definitely revisit this place.< /Review>

1/30/20 Edit: after their vacation, I decided to give them a real chance and try their food. Should have just left it as is...

Had the $40 deluxe sushi lunch and had one otoro and one butterfish for additional $17.

Some of the sushi definitely had a super fishy taste when at most other places, there isn‚Äôt normally any. Some of the pieces were chewy when they usually wouldn‚Äôt be (like the butterfish). The rice was hard and most of the nigiri fell apart (bad rice quality).

The otoro has really good flavor but not butchered properly, still had the fleshy part in my friend‚Äôs piece.

1/23/20
Really wanted to come try but if you close your restaurant for two random weeks not during a holiday season and don‚Äôt post about it on google maps or yelp, there‚Äôs an issue. I actually made a trip to come out and even when you show up, there‚Äôs just a tiny tiny sign that says they‚Äôre closed.

That‚Äôs a bad customer experience right there
(I showed up around 1:00 on Thursday, when they are scheduled to be open).</Review>

< Review>
One of the best Japanese restaurants I have visited in SF!!
Ordered the mystery chirashi box, which comes in 9 mini chirashi bowls, and tea braised octopus. The ingredients are super fresh and you can taste each individual unique flavor and texture. The seasoning was very creative and really goes well with the food. The yuzu wasabi and the nori rice flakes were our favourites! The tea braised octupus was really impressive and we loved how it was chewy and tender at the same time!
Other items on the menu was also intriguing, such as the omasake, starters, sushi, etc. Will definitely come back!
The ambience of the restaurant was nice, warm and cozy. Would suggest making reservation before coming. The staffs were quick and friendly, and they explain everything when serving.< /Review>

< Review>
My first time to this Taqueria, I was in a mood for a quesadilla. I originally ordered a super quesadilla but the gentleman at the counter took a moment to explain to me the different kind of quesadillas they have, they have an original one that is only meat and cheese, they have the super which is meat, cheese, guacamole, and sour cream and the have the Los Gallos which is meat, cheese, guacamole, sour cream, lettuce and tomato which is what I wanted. I appreciate the gentleman with white hair informing me, that's great customer service in my book. I also order a small horchata, once you are done paying you go to the left through the arched opening than an immediate right and you will see all the drinks.
Their chips and salsa are really good, I hope they will make a green salsa soon, the facility is very clean.

They have earned my business I will be a regular here the food was really good and the flavoring was perfect.

I highly recommend, Management keep up the good work!<//Review>

<review>I used to drive by this place and would occasionally see a line outside the door. I finally decide to stop in and see what the fuss was about.
Besides the place being a bit small, the food is really what the line is about! Everything I've had has so much flavor and is so good!
They do not skimp on the portions (see the photos to better understand) and I think the prices are pretty good for the portions. I've tried the Super Burritos and I rarely finish them in one sitting. I've also had the Super Nachos with meat and they make a good leftover meal as well. I have not yet tried it but they also serve Menudo on the weekends (maybe Sundays only).
They have a pretty good menu size as well as serving breakfast meals. there are so many things I want to try still!
Now my only complaint is the salsa bar. First, there are no signs to tell you which is which or the hotness of each one. Second, the mild salsa doesn't always look or taste fresh. I tend to stay away from the salsa bar unless it is early in the day and I can be reasonable sure it is fresh. Other than that, I still return and I've always satisfied!</review>< Pictures>

< Review>
I will always try and rate this place 5 stars when I can. I've been going here all my life. Since when I could start eating beans (most babies would eat apple sauce!) So about 26 years I've been coming here. Lately, the last couple times tho...I understand people come and go staff wise, you have to stay on top with the cost of living but plates are getting up there in price! I absolutely love the plain quesadillas, shrimp cocktail, al pastor plate, Carne asada plate, their guac, etc. I hear their aguas are good too.

Anyway, as of this year, 2019, there have been some notable changes in the food. I hope it was just the last two times because I will always come here with my parents whenever I can. Its just a great go-to Mexican spot in Newark!</Review>

Lumpers are available for a fee, so bring a com check with you. Lunch truck comes around every few hours so your not starving. Overall a decent facility. There are bathroom /port a potties available for drivers.< /review>

<user_id>109681695903583202747< /user_id><user_name>Monica<//user_name>< Date>

< rating>

<Review>I had an amazing experience visiting Rooky's for the first time. Upon arrival I was blown away by the mass qtys of 45s, which is what I came in looking for. I was warmly greeted by the owner, who asked me if I was looking for anything specific.
I was a bit overwhelmed by how much there was so him directing me to the area he thought I might best find what I wanted (he was right) I started digging!
Within the first 90 mims I had pulled at least 20 of interest, before having to run out and feed my meter. (You know it's a good dog when you have to feed your meter several times in one trip!)
Once I realized how long I had been in there I decided to stop digging and make my final selections. Besides the more expensive records for sale- all which were priced $5 or $10- there was also three times as many for sale priced at 3/$5.
After dbl checking my discogs where I have all my records I own inventoried (no more duplicate purchases- yay!) I narrowed my final selection down to 12 which I was super happy with. The best part was that four of them were ones on my wishlist!!
When I went to pay, the wonderful owner mentioned that I could bring him a wishlist and he'd be happy to see if he had any of them, which I thought was so great!
Besides how huge of a selection and the fair pricing, it was the kindness and helpfulness of the owner that really impressed me most. He was very sweet and genuinely wanted to help me and not just to make a quick sale. I mean this bc when I was about to pay, I asked him what Styrene meant. He explained the easiest way to tell and explained how vinyl esp motown would wear out over many plays, and suggested that I listen to a stevie wonder 45 I had in my hands just to be sure it was still in good playable cond. So he took me over to the turntables and showed me how to properly use it to  DBL check my selections, which I did. As a result, I put 3 of my 12 back. And even though he might have lost $5 on my total sale that day, his honesty and helpfulness will keep me coming back now again and again!
Overall it was a hugely positive 3 hour shopping experience, and I can't wait for my next dig!!<//Review>< pics>

[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPVNzsSIm-PEdBtzd0yCkssgwxhxCv3yJzgHveu=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP93QD0uyjqmp1byzVNlDIIwdsIG3uUplMQNXLl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics>

< date>
1552759438382<//date>
< review>
If you are looking for vinyl this is the place to go. On a typical day, if you're at the listening station, you'll see the oddest selection of the Buying and Selling vinyl cognoscenti slink in and out of the back room as they work their dark deals. Good news though: The scraps left behind by these apex predators are an eclectic and fascinating mix of old and new Soul, Funk, Gospel, Blues - Rock and Proto-Rock and at fair prices.  Somehow I ended up with the new Nick Waterhouse (Self Titled) LP - and it wasn't even available yet online.

Word of warning though - the proprietor is not a patient man and should be approached cautiously - he really knows his stuff, but if you walk in there in your favorite loafers and no socks - and start musing about how well 'curated' the place is, you are looking for trouble (as I learned).

When I saw that the local game in the back room is Cassino - I decided flex my card tactics to recover my honor. I was soundly put in my place there too -  but ended up with a nice branded felt slip mat for my trouble.< /review>
< user_name>
Stuart Fox</user_name>
</record>

<UserId.>107136176059594037309<//UserId.><Name>Luis P.< /Name>< date>
1411146393156<//date>
<rate>3</rate><Review>Perhaps it is time to admit that looking for a great pizza might be a fruitless task. After all the pizza searching and eating in California, all we have accomplished is a half wanted result. Even Mozza which claims the higher prices, known as a high end pizzeria was truly unremarkable, but certainly expensive, with only small size pizzas and a serious lack of ingredients, they thought they were superior than the rest because they throw fresh herbs in their creations.
Enter Times Square New York Style Pizzeria in Temecula, CA, yet one more franchise in the ever expanding world of pizza making. This is where the waters get a little murky, when you hear the advertisement that this is authentic New York Style Pizza. First of all, I have yet to go to New York in person, but I have seen countless programs of their deli, pizza and quality restaurants. At the end of the day this is what New York Style pizza means to us: nice thin dough, plenty dry but since it is thin it passes muster (barely), a serious small amount of ingredient seems to be the official trademark of New York Style Pizza, maybe that is the reason why New Yorkers fold the pizza lengthwise (knows too many as the correct way to eat this pizza), and since it is barely laden with righteous ingredients, is kind of like eating bread more than anything else. I am sure those that review this pizza as the authentic item are, either from New York (therefore their strong defense for all things New York), or easily impressed by a pizza that in all seriousness lack about 40 to 50 % more toppings. We had the following pizzas avid for the best:
Pepperoni, 17 inches, $14.99: Not one of the aspects of the pizza was remarkable, perhaps the thinness the only true positive point, but that is about is. If there was cheese it must have gone back to where it was made for we had to let the imagination convince us of its presence. Pepperoni, another one of those toppings with no heart and soul, which is the one of the main problems of the pizza business: sub par toppings. 3 Stars.
NY Style White Pizza, 17 inches, $16.99: it seems that in this place 17 inch is the only size they carry, which in a way dispels the need to ponder and fret for what size to get. This one had the same lack of ingredients, just folded in two and nothing drips, and to our shock, for lack of a better word, a mound of pizza sauce right on the middle of the made pizza. How gourmet, considering that their sauce is nothing to write home about! Imagine that, ask for a white pizza but their delicate sense of taste throw in a big mound of pizza sauce. The other ingredients were: mozzarella cheese, ricotta, garlic, garnished with pizza sauce, parmesan, basil and oregano. Sounds like a lot of ingredients, eh? Not to be so, just a sprinkle here and there so you can fold it as well and eat it while you walk down the busy streets of New York. 3 Stars.
Do not get me wrong. I understand cost in a restaurant business, but one thing is cost, and another total thing is lack of ingredients and a dough that is thin but dry.
Service was adequate in that we took these pizzas to go. Perhaps it is time to look at the frozen section a little more closely if one is near home, and wanting a great pizza! 3 Stars.< /Review>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>

None<//resp>

< review>
I live in Martinez so maybe I'm a little biased but my daughter who is at the Actors Studio in NY did a show with the cast here and she loved it. It's a cute little theater in downtown Martinez with a fantastic bar when you walk in and a whole lot of personality. The staff is fabulous and the acting is Awesome!! They have actors who have worked in Hollywood and in NY and the shows are so well written and acted. Engaging, entertaining, and just plain fun. If you haven't been here find a play that looks fun and go, I promise you'll love it.<//review>

< name>
cp leblow</name>
< Date>
1549814629820< /Date>
<rate>5<//rate>< Review>
Marvelous little theater in downtown Martinez one block off of Main Street and close to restaurants and bars. On a rainy, cold Saturday night there was plenty of free street parking but I would imagine it can be more congested depending on the time of year. The theater staff was friendly and polite and the lobby inside was warm and cozy. Wine, coffee and assorted snacks were offered for sale. Our party of four was here for a play, "White Guy on the Bus". The theater inside was smaller than I expected with fairly steep stadium seating. Not a bad seat in the house. The production was professionally staged and performed by local thespians and brought to this theater by WOW (Women of Wonder). My daughter who just moved to Martinez turned us on to this gem. We will definitely return for more little theater productions in the future.</Review>

< review>
Best place in the Delta for breakfast, lunch, and dinner. The staff is awesome and personable. Your money and time will not be wasted. Remember this, Sylvia's is not a fast food joint. This place can get packed fast on the weekends between 11am to 1pm so plan well. They have a wide variety of food for kids and some great desserts. The seatings are comfortable and the ambiance is definitely country; however, the restaurant clientele is diverse. Experience Sylvia's and you experience love.</review>

< Text>
The waitress was excellent, but it was getting seated by the manager that was the problem.  She needs to be reprimanded.

We had a reservation at 11am, and did not get seated until about one hour later, just before noon.  Yes, that's right NOON!  We were being continually told by the manager, who was seating people that morning that our table was being cleaned off, or the current guests were just wrapping it up, only to find out that was not the case.  Or maybe it was, and everyone around us was being seated.  Then I was told that our table was ready and they were cleaning it off, she even pointed to it, only to see her seat a family there ahead of us.....that is when I came unglued, and started having words with the manager, who then told me that I should probably just leave.  Yes, she said leave the restaurant.  Unbelievable.  This was the manager of the store.

She is there to serve us, and if she doesn't want to do it fairly, and without lying to us, then she should just retire from her job.

I expect the owner to request that she give us an apology, and I will not accept anything less than that.</Text>

This is one of the best places to eat in Antioch!  They have huge portions.  I always save one half for later.

My favorite is the French toast. It's Texas toast which is thick and large.  I use strawberry jam instead of syrup.  My Mom used to make it that way when I was kid:).

I also like their Cobb salad with grilled chicken!  Amazing!  Did I mention the breakfast burrito?  There's a ton to chose from.  There's also that good old fashion eggs and bacon!  Anything you order will be excellent!

I order to go a lot.  I know the number by heart!  That's scary!  Thank God this place doesn't recognize my voice!  They're also on Yelp's eat24 for delivery.

Only 4 stars because this place is so popular you need to wait, during busy weekend breakfast, nearly 30 mins for a table everytime we visit.  Their portions are huge.  I feel (because I'm a business owner myself) the amount of waste must be atrocious.  It was almost unappetizing the plate was so over-filled.  Food was  fantastic.  We ordered for a family of 5.
